When an event is observed in one variable, SharpBayes propagates this evidence to all other variables in the network.\r\nTasks like classification, regression, anomaly detection, prediction and diagnostics can all be performed using Bayesian networks.\r\nInfluence Diagrams extend the usability of bayesian networks by incorporating the concept of Decision and Utility nodes.
